  margin: 0;
  padding: 0;

  font: inherit;
  font-size: 100%;
  vertical-align: baseline; }

  line-height: 1; }

  border-collapse: collapse;
  border-spacing: 0; }

  text-align: left;
  font-weight: normal;
  vertical-align: middle; }

  quotes: none; }

  content: "";
